The gooey molds were probably the result of a chemical incompatibility.  Check the silicone that stayed gooey and see if it's platinum cure (platsil).  If it is that means the Apoxy Sculpt probably has sulfur in it.  Sulfur and platinum silicone don't play well together.  Make sure you use tin cure silicone instead.  Sulfur doesn't bother tin cure silicone. That'd be my guess.
